- Secret hygiene contract: 8 secret patterns × 4 audit-side artefacts = **32 проверок отсутствия leak** на каждый PR.
- Backward compatibility: feature-gated — `MCP_NOTIFICATIONS_ENABLED=false` (default) полностью отключает webhook subsystem; rate limiter с `memory` backend не требует Redis. Existing `tools/call` flow без auth changes.
- Determinism: `target_redacted = sha256(url)[:12]` детерминирован; circuit breaker — in-process state, restart очищает (correct semantics для transient upstream failures); rate limiter clock-injectable для tests.

### Added (ARG-032 — Cycle 4: Per-tool parsers batch 4 — browser/binary/recon/auth, +30 parsers, 2026-04-19)

- **30 новых per-tool parsers** (mapped 68 → **98**, heartbeat 89 → **59**, DoD §19.6 catalog coverage **62.4 %**, +14.4 п.п. vs Cycle 3 ARG-029) — каждый pure-function `parse_<tool>(stdout, stderr, artifacts_dir, tool_id) → list[FindingDTO]` поверх существующих `_base.py` / `_text_base.py` / `_jsonl_base.py` / `_browser_base.py` / `_subdomain_base.py` / `_credential_base.py` фундаментов. Среднее ≈ 220 LoC, hard cap 350 LoC, single-responsibility decomposition (severity normaliser → category classifier → finding builder → sidecar emitter), детерминированный `stable_hash_12((target, location, rule_id, severity))` per finding.
- **Batch 4a — Browser (6 tools, 0 % → 100 % browser-coverage):** `playwright_runner` / `puppeteer_screens` (HAR + screenshot manifest, JSON_OBJECT), `chrome_csp_probe` (CSP violation report → MISCONFIG), `webanalyze` (Wappalyzer-style detection → INFO с CVSS=0), `gowitness` (screenshot manifest), `whatweb` (technology fingerprint). **Critical security gate:** все шесть прогоняют HAR через единый `_browser_base.iter_har_entries`, который вырезает заголовки `Cookie` / `Set-Cookie` / `Authorization` / `Proxy-Authorization` (заменяет каноничным маркером, не дропает entry — оператор видит, что header был), редактирует `request.url` через `redact_password_in_text` (URL-embedded `user:pw@host` → `[REDACTED-PASSWORD]@host`), маскирует `postData.text` до длинного маркера (`bodyLength` сохраняется для триажа). Найден и исправлен **прод-баг в Python 3.12+ `urllib.parse.urlsplit`**: после инъекции маркера в userinfo netloc становится bracket-invalid и парсер падает `ValueError`; новый helper `_browser_base.safe_url_parts()` отрезает credential-фрагмент **до** парсинга, host/path извлекаются стабильно, дальнейший redact идёт на чистом URL.
- **Batch 4b — Binary (4 tools) + Subdomain recon (6 tools):** `radare2_info` (compound `r2 -j` JSON: imports/sections/strings — flagging dangerous functions / `rwx` sections / high-entropy), `apktool` (Android manifest warnings → MISCONFIG: `debuggable=true`, `allowBackup=true`, `cleartextTrafficPermitted=true`), `binwalk` (signature offsets — `private key` / `RSA private key` / `OpenSSH private key` сигнатуры → MISCONFIG, остальное → INFO), `jadx` (decompiler ERROR/WARN lines → CONFIG_DRIFT). **Critical security gate** для всех четырёх: memory addresses (`0x[0-9a-fA-F]{8,}`) систематически прогоняются через `scrub_evidence_strings` → `[REDACTED-ADDR]` перед sidecar persistence — ASLR offset'ы НЕ leak'аются. Subdomain recon: `amass_passive` / `subfinder` (JSONL), `assetfinder` / `findomain` / `chaos` (TEXT_LINES), `dnsrecon` (JSON_OBJECT с `records[]`), `fierce` (JSON_OBJECT с `found_dns[]` + `zone_transfer.successful=true` → MISCONFIG escalation). Все семь делят `_subdomain_base.is_valid_hostname` (RFC-1035 LDH validation) — noise lines типа `[+] processing example.com` или `NOT VALID` дропаются ДО построения FindingDTO.
- **Batch 4c — Credential bruteforce / NTLM relay (8 tools) + Network/OSINT/probes (6 tools):** `hydra` / `medusa` / `patator` / `ncrack` (text bruteforce output, single-source-of-truth `_credential_base.build_credential_finding` + `build_credential_evidence`), `crackmapexec` (CME success line `<PROTO> <HOST> <PORT> <NETBIOS> [+] <DOMAIN>\<USER>:<CRED>`, отдельный path для cleartext vs NTLM `LM:NT` 32:32 hex hash pair), `responder` (NTLMv1 / NTLMv2-SSP capture lines, отдельные ветки для протоколов), `hashcat` (cracked rows: cleartext, MD5, bcrypt, NTLM), `ntlmrelayx` (relay success + SAM dump). **Critical security gate (defence-in-depth, четыре уровня):** (1) cleartext password — replaced with `[REDACTED-PASSWORD]` + `password_length: int` hint; (2) NTLM `LM:NT` pair (`[a-fA-F0-9]{32}:[a-fA-F0-9]{32}`) — replaced with `REDACTED_NT_HASH_MARKER`; (3) NTLMv1 / NTLMv2 hash blob (`server::domain:challenge:proof:hmac`) — replaced with `redact_hash_string` marker, сохраняется тип хеша + username + fingerprint hash; (4) bootkey / SAM hash dump — replaced inline. Network/probes: `dnsx` (JSONL DNS resolver — wildcard SOA/TXT escalation), `chaos` (ProjectDiscovery passive subdomains), `censys` (services per IP), `mongodb_probe` / `redis_cli_probe` (auth-required gating: `auth_required: false` → HIGH MISCONFIG), `unicornscan` (TCP/UDP open lines).
- **Dispatch wiring** в `src/sandbox/parsers/__init__.py::_DEFAULT_TOOL_PARSERS` — добавлены 30 entries в существующий dict; ни один YAML/SIGNATURES не тронут. `get_registered_tool_parsers()` после Cycle 4 batch 4 возвращает frozenset размером **98** — фиксируется в новом `test_registered_count_is_98` integration-тесте (regression brake).
- **Coverage matrix ratchet** — `tests/test_tool_catalog_coverage.py::MAPPED_PARSER_COUNT` 68 → **98**, `HEARTBEAT_PARSER_COUNT` 89 → **59**, ratchet identifier-set `_ARG029_NEWLY_MAPPED` → `_ARG032_NEWLY_MAPPED` (содержит 30 свежих tool_ids). Тест `test_parser_coverage_counts_match_arg032_ratchet` упадёт, если кто-то снова уронит mapped < 98 или heartbeat > 59.
- **C11 (parser determinism) + C12 (evidence redaction completeness)** контракты из ARG-030 авто-покрывают все 30 новых парсеров без правки самих контрактов; `_C12_KNOWN_LEAKERS` остаётся **пустым** — ни один из 30 парсеров не утекает baseline blob через свой sidecar. Determinism: 30 × `test_arg032_dispatch_is_deterministic[<tool>]` (run twice, byte-identical sidecar) — все green.
- **Integration suite `tests/integration/sandbox/parsers/test_arg032_dispatch.py` (NEW)** — **149 параметрических кейсов** (30 регистрация + 30 routing + 30 sidecar + 30 determinism + 18 critical security + 7 hostname-validator + sanity + multi-tool isolation): (i) `test_arg032_tool_is_registered[<tool>]`, (ii) `test_dispatch_routes_each_arg032_tool[<tool>]`, (iii) `test_dispatch_writes_per_tool_sidecar[<tool>]`, (iv) `test_arg032_dispatch_is_deterministic[<tool>]`, (v) `test_browser_har_strips_cookie_and_auth_headers[playwright_runner|puppeteer_screens]`, (vi) `test_browser_url_credentials_redacted[puppeteer_screens|gowitness|whatweb]`, (vii) `test_binary_parsers_redact_memory_addresses[radare2_info|binwalk|jadx]`, (viii) `test_credential_parsers_redact_cleartext_password[hydra|medusa|patator|ncrack|crackmapexec]`, (ix) `test_ntlm_hash_redaction[responder|hashcat|ntlmrelayx|crackmapexec]`, (x) `test_subdomain_parsers_drop_noise_lines[<7 tools>]`, (xi) `test_arg032_does_not_drop_prior_cycle_registrations` (sample 27 ARG-021/-022/-029 tools survives), (xii) `test_arg032_tools_use_distinct_sidecar_filenames` (no overwrite в shared `/out`), (xiii) `test_heartbeat_fallback_for_unmapped_tool_id`, (xiv) `test_all_arg032_parsers_in_single_artifacts_dir_keeps_sidecars_intact`. Inline bait blobs (`_HAR_COOKIE_BAIT`, `_HAR_AUTH_BAIT`, `_MEMORY_ADDR_BAIT`, `_NTLM_HASH_BAIT`, `_PASSWORD_BAIT`) дают одностраничный регрешн-локус: любая будущая правка парсера, которая снова утечёт секрет, упадёт ровно в этом файле.
- **Unit suite (NEW per-tool):** **225 unit-тестов** распределены по 30 модулям (среднее 7.5 теста/парсер, минимум 6, максимум 12). Покрытие per-module branch ≥ 90 %.
- **`docs/tool-catalog.md`** — регенерирован через `python -m scripts.docs_tool_catalog --out ../docs/tool-catalog.md`; header summary теперь показывает Mapped: **98 (62.4 %)**, Heartbeat: **59 (37.6 %)** на 157 tool descriptors. `--check` mode: drift = 0.

### Metrics (ARG-032)

- Файлов создано: **30** parser-модулей (`backend/src/sandbox/parsers/<tool>_parser.py`) + **30** unit-test файлов (`backend/tests/unit/sandbox/parsers/test_<tool>_parser.py`) + **1** integration suite (`tests/integration/sandbox/parsers/test_arg032_dispatch.py`).
- Файлов изменено: **5** (`backend/src/sandbox/parsers/__init__.py` — registry +30 entries, `backend/src/sandbox/parsers/_browser_base.py` — `safe_url_parts` helper + `urlsplit` Python-3.12 fix, `backend/tests/test_tool_catalog_coverage.py` — ratchet 68→98 / 89→59 + `_ARG032_NEWLY_MAPPED` set, `docs/tool-catalog.md` — auto-regen, `CHANGELOG.md`).
- Mapped parsers: 68 → **98** (+30, +44 %). Heartbeat: 89 → **59** (-30, -34 %). DoD §19.6 catalog coverage: 43.3 % → **62.4 %** (+19.1 п.п.).

### Added (ARG-031 — Cycle 4: Valhalla tier renderer + business-impact lens, 2026-04-19)

- **`backend/src/reports/valhalla_tier_renderer.py` (NEW, ~1 030 LoC)** — третий и финальный ReportService tier (Midgard 12/18 → Valhalla **18/18**). Чистая функция `assemble_valhalla_sections(scan_data, business_context, sanitize_context, presigner) → ValhallaSectionAssembly` строит frozen Pydantic-сборку с фиксированным порядком разделов: `title_meta`, `executive_summary`, `executive_summary_counts`, `risk_quantification_per_asset`, `owasp_rollup_matrix`, `top_findings_by_business_impact`, `remediation_roadmap`, `evidence_refs`, `timeline_entries`. Все sub-models (`AssetRiskRow`, `OwaspRollupRow`, `BusinessImpactFindingRow`, `RemediationPhaseRow`, `ValhallaEvidenceRef`, `ValhallaTimelineEntry`) — `frozen=True`, `extra="forbid"`, детерминированный порядок полей.
- **Risk quantification per asset** — composite score `max(cvss_v3) × business_value_weight × exploitability_factor`, сортировка по убыванию, cap = 50 строк. `BusinessContext` (новая публичная Pydantic-модель) принимает `(host, weight)` mapping; при отсутствии — fallback на `default_business_value` (1.0). Asset выводится из `proof_of_concept.url` / `target` через детерминированный URL-парсер (host без порта).
- **OWASP Top-10 (2025) rollup matrix** — стабильная сетка `A01..A10` + `A00` (Other / Unmapped) × {critical, high, medium, low, info}. Категория finding'а определяется приоритетом `Finding.owasp_category` → CWE→OWASP-2025 mapping → `A00`. Mapping table покрывает 30+ CWE (CWE-79 → A05, CWE-22 → A01, CWE-89 → A05, CWE-287 → A07, CWE-200/798 → A07, CWE-502 → A08 и т.д.) — расширяется через `_CWE_TO_OWASP_2025` в самом модуле без правки YAML.
- **Top-N findings by business impact** (cap = 25) — sort key `(-composite, severity_rank, tool_id, root_cause_hash)` для детерминированного tie-breaking. Каждая reproducer/replay_command аргумент-цепочка прогоняется через `sanitize_replay_command(argv, sanitize_ctx)` и сохраняется в `BusinessImpactFindingRow.sanitized_command` — executive увидит, что секреты были вычищены до того, как CISO/Board открыли отчёт.
- **Auto-generated executive summary** — детерминированный template fill (`"During scan {scan_id} for tenant {tenant_id} as of {timestamp}, ARGUS identified {N} finding(s) ({critical} CRITICAL, {high} HIGH, …). Top business risk: {asset} (composite score {score}). Recommended priority: {phase}."`). LLM путь намеренно НЕ default — он сломает byte-stable snapshot контракт. Feature flag `ARGUS_VALHALLA_LLM_SUMMARY` зарезервирован под Cycle 5.
- **Remediation roadmap** — четырёхфазное bucketing: P0 (critical, SLA ≤ 7 days), P1 (high, SLA ≤ 30 days), P2 (medium, SLA ≤ 90 days), P3 (low/info, backlog). Каждая фаза несёт `phase_id`, `sla_days`, `severity_bucket`, `finding_count`, `top_finding_titles` (≤ 5).
- **Evidence references** — поддержка опционального `presigner: Callable[[str], str | None]` callback (mirror Asgard). При отсутствии presigner'а `presigned_url=None`, шаблон корректно рендерит fallback. Каждая запись сохраняет `finding_id`, `object_key`, `description`, `presigned_url`.
- **Pipeline timeline** — chronological extract из `ReportData.timeline`; снэпшот компактный, без полного `entry`-payload (только `phase`, `order_index`, `created_at`, JSON-snippet ≤ 80 chars).
- **`backend/src/reports/tier_classifier.py`** — `_project_valhalla` переписан с pass-through на defence-in-depth: каждый finding прогоняется через `_sanitise_finding(f, sanitize_ctx=…)` ПЕРЕД попаданием в `assemble_valhalla_sections`, гарантируя, что любой раннер, минующий sanitiser, всё равно получит чистый payload. **Bonus**: `_project_midgard` тоже теперь sanitises — purely additive, idempotent — закрывает defence-in-depth gap (Midgard JSON всё ещё surfaces `proof_of_concept`).
- **`backend/src/reports/report_service.py`** — `render_bundle(business_context: BusinessContext | None = None, ...)` параметр пропихнут до `assemble_valhalla_sections`. `_build_jinja_context` обзавелся новой VALHALLA-веткой, проектирующей `valhalla_assembly` через `valhalla_assembly_to_jinja_context(...)` в Jinja-context под ключом `valhalla_executive_report`. Old-style `valhalla_report` (operator view) сохранен — namespace бок-о-бок без коллизий.
- **`backend/src/reports/generators.py::generate_json`** — VALHALLA-ветка emit'ит `valhalla_executive_report` под отдельным ключом параллельно legacy `valhalla_report`. `_canonical_json_nested` гарантирует sort_keys + (',', ':') separator + LF newline, что обеспечивает byte-stable snapshot.
- **`backend/src/reports/templates/reports/partials/valhalla/executive_report.html.j2` (NEW)** — single-partial рендер всего executive раздела: title meta-grid, summary card, severity counts pills, asset risk table, OWASP rollup matrix, top findings table (с колонкой `sanitized_command`), remediation roadmap grid (P0..P3 cards), evidence table, timeline table, footer. Inline CSS scoped to `.valhalla-exec` — gold (`#c9a64a`) on dark-grey (`#1f1f24`/`#2a2a30`), не перекрывает остальные стили. `valhalla.html.j2::extra` block `{% include %}` partial'а; legacy `valhalla_context` не тронут — backward compatible.
- **`backend/src/reports/__init__.py`** — экспортированы `ValhallaSectionAssembly`, `assemble_valhalla_sections`, `valhalla_assembly_to_jinja_context`, `BusinessContext`, `AssetRiskRow`, `OwaspRollupRow`, `BusinessImpactFindingRow`, `RemediationPhaseRow`, `ValhallaEvidenceRef`, `ValhallaTimelineEntry`, `VALHALLA_EXECUTIVE_SECTION_ORDER`, `VALHALLA_TOP_FINDINGS_CAP`, `VALHALLA_TOP_ASSETS_CAP`.
- **`backend/tests/unit/reports/test_valhalla_tier_renderer.py` (NEW, 48 cases)** — покрытие: assembly determinism (run twice, byte-identical model_dump), section ordering invariants, sanitiser threading через reproducer/replay_command, business-context propagation в composite score, OWASP rollup correctness (CWE-79→A05, CWE-287→A07, CWE-22→A01, unmapped→A00), evidence presigning, executive summary template (empty/single/multiple findings), edge cases (zero findings, missing CVSS, missing CWE), Pydantic frozen-model immutability (попытка set existing field на каждом из 6 row-моделей даёт TypeError/AttributeError).
- **`backend/tests/integration/reports/test_valhalla_tier_all_formats.py` (NEW, 27 PASS / 2 SKIP)** — все 6 форматов (HTML / PDF / JSON / CSV / SARIF / JUnit), bundle sha256 verification, no-secret-leak regex sweep по 8 forbidden literals + 8 regex patterns на каждый из 5 текстовых форматов, sanitiser placeholder visibility (HTML + JSON), `valhalla_executive_report` blob present in JSON, top findings ranked по business value (`payments.acme.example.com` × 5.0 ranks #1), tier isolation (Midgard и Asgard НЕ emit'ят `valhalla_executive_report`), assembly round-trip determinism, byte-identical bundle across runs, snapshot byte-equality для 5 текстовых форматов, structural snapshot для PDF (skip-on-missing-WeasyPrint).
- **5 byte-stable snapshots** (`backend/tests/snapshots/reports/valhalla_canonical.{html,json,csv,sarif,xml}`) — захвачены через `$env:ARGUS_SNAPSHOT_REFRESH = "1"; pytest tests/integration/reports/test_valhalla_tier_all_formats.py -m ""`. Любой template-/context-drift даст немедленную diff-failure в integration suite.
- **`backend/tests/security/test_report_no_secret_leak.py`** — security gate расширен с **Asgard-only (275 cases)** до полной матрицы **Midgard + Asgard + Valhalla × 6 форматов × 55 patterns = 990 cases** (1 056 общих с auxiliary tests). PDF-rows skip gracefully на хостах без WeasyPrint (CI WeasyPrint job — green). Добавлен defence-in-depth для Midgard через `_project_midgard` — закрывает leak для всех 55 patterns в Midgard JSON (раньше surface'ил raw secrets через `proof_of_concept`).
- **`docs/report-service.md`** — добавлен новый раздел `## ARG-031 — Valhalla tier`: tier diff matrix Midgard ↔ Asgard ↔ Valhalla, branded template recipe, full JSON contract пример с `valhalla_executive_report` блоком, Valhalla rendering API code sample (с `BusinessContext`), snapshot regen recipe, security gate extension docs.

### Metrics (ARG-031)

- Файлов создано: **3** (`backend/src/reports/valhalla_tier_renderer.py`, `backend/src/reports/templates/reports/partials/valhalla/executive_report.html.j2`, `backend/tests/integration/reports/test_valhalla_tier_all_formats.py`) + **1** unit test (`backend/tests/unit/reports/test_valhalla_tier_renderer.py`) + **5** snapshot файлов.
- Файлов изменено: **6** (`backend/src/reports/tier_classifier.py`, `backend/src/reports/report_service.py`, `backend/src/reports/generators.py`, `backend/src/reports/__init__.py`, `backend/src/reports/templates/reports/valhalla.html.j2`, `backend/tests/security/test_report_no_secret_leak.py`, `docs/report-service.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`).

### Added (ARG-039 — Cycle 4: MCP OpenAPI 3.1 export + TypeScript SDK + docstring CI gate, 2026-04-19)

- **`backend/src/mcp/openapi_emitter.py` (NEW, ~310 LoC)** — детерминированный pure-function эмиттер `build_openapi_spec(app: FastMCP) -> dict[str, Any]`. Обходит весь capability surface FastMCP-приложения (15 tools + 4 resources + 0 templates + 3 prompts на момент Cycle 4) через публичные async-методы (`list_tools`, `list_resources`, `list_resource_templates`, `list_prompts`), маппит каждую entity на каноничный OpenAPI 3.1 path: `@mcp.tool("x.y") → POST /rpc/x.y` (operationId `call_x_y`, тег `mcp-tool`), `@mcp.resource("argus://x/y") → GET /resources/x/y` (operationId `read_argus_x_y`, тег `mcp-resource`), `argus://x/{id}` template → `GET /resources/x/{id}` с явно объявленным path-параметром, `@mcp.prompt("x.y") → POST /prompts/x.y` (operationId `render_x_y`, тег `mcp-prompt`). Pydantic-схемы из `inputSchema` / `outputSchema` поднимаются из локальных `$defs` в глобальный `components.schemas`, все `$ref` рекурсивно переписываются с `#/$defs/X` на `#/components/schemas/X` — спецификация самодостаточна (любой строгий валидатор OpenAPI 3.1 и `openapi-typescript-codegen` резолвят все ссылки без доступа к Pydantic-моделям). Аргументы prompts синтезируются в JSON Schema (`{Name}PromptArguments`), сортируются по ключу — детерминированный YAML-снэпшот.
- **`backend/scripts/export_mcp_openapi.py` (NEW)** — CLI с двумя режимами: `--out <path>` (regenerate) и `--check` (CI-гейт, exit 1 при дрейфе). Сериализация — `yaml.safe_dump(sort_keys=True, allow_unicode=False, default_flow_style=False, width=120)` + LF newlines — байт-в-байт идентичный output на Windows / Linux / macOS.
- **`docs/mcp-server-openapi.yaml` (NEW, 68 KB / ~2 700 LoC)** — закоммиченный snapshot спецификации, source of truth для интеграторов и SDK-генератора. Покрывает 22 path / 65 schemas / 2 securitySchemes (`bearer` + `apiKey`).
- **`Frontend/package.json`** — добавлена pinned dev-зависимость `openapi-typescript-codegen@0.29.0` (точная версия, без `^`/`~`) + два npm-скрипта: `sdk:generate` (полная регенерация `Frontend/src/sdk/argus-mcp/`) и `sdk:check` (`sdk:generate` + `git diff --exit-code` против закоммиченного состояния, exit 1 при дрейфе). Параметры кодогена: `--client fetch --useUnionTypes --useOptions --indent 2`.
- **`Frontend/src/sdk/argus-mcp/` (NEW, 75 файлов / ~74 KB)** — auto-generated TypeScript SDK с тремя сервис-классами (`McpToolService`, `McpResourceService`, `McpPromptService`) и моделями для каждой Pydantic-схемы из спецификации. Frontend `npx tsc --noEmit` — clean (SDK интегрируется без правок tsconfig / без shim-типов).
- **`backend/tests/test_mcp_tools_have_docstrings.py` (NEW)** — параметризованный CI-гейт: каждый зарегистрированный tool / resource / resource template / prompt обязан иметь поле `description` ≥ 30 символов (это поле, а не Python `__doc__`, попадает в OpenAPI и SDK). 23 теста (15 tools + 4 resources + 3 prompts + 1 sanity) — все зелёные, ни одного inline-фикса не потребовалось (предыдущие циклы ARG-023…ARG-029 уже пишут полноценные descriptions).
- **`backend/tests/integration/mcp/test_openapi_export_stable.py` (NEW)** — 6 интеграционных снэпшот-инвариантов: (1) committed YAML round-trips byte-for-byte с `build_openapi_spec(build_app())`, (2) валидность OpenAPI 3.1 metadata + `securitySchemes`, (3) coverage всех runtime-entity (каждый tool/resource/template/prompt → path), (4) каждый `$ref` резолвится в `components.schemas`, никаких leaked `#/$defs/*` ссылок, (5) каждая `POST /rpc/*` имеет `operationId call_*`, requestBody-`$ref`, responses 200/401, (6) каждая `POST /prompts/*` ссылается на синтезированный `{Name}PromptArguments` schema.
- **`backend/tests/conftest.py`** — `_OFFLINE_FILE_NAMES` расширен двумя новыми именами (`test_mcp_tools_have_docstrings.py`, `test_openapi_export_stable.py`) — оба теста pure-Python introspection без БД/брокера, поэтому корректно классифицируются как offline и попадают в default `pytest -q` без флага `requires_docker`.
- **`.github/workflows/ci.yml`** — новый job `mcp-openapi-drift` (run-after-pull-request, добавлен в `needs:` для `build`). Шаги: (a) Python 3.12 + backend deps, (b) `python -m scripts.export_mcp_openapi --check` (drift на спецификации), (c) `pytest tests/test_mcp_tools_have_docstrings.py` (docstring gate), (d) Node 20 + `npm ci` (Frontend), (e) `npm run sdk:check` (drift на SDK). Любой из четырёх steps падает exit 1 → блокирует merge.

### Metrics (ARG-039)

- Файлов создано: **5** (`backend/src/mcp/openapi_emitter.py`, `backend/scripts/export_mcp_openapi.py`, `docs/mcp-server-openapi.yaml`, `backend/tests/test_mcp_tools_have_docstrings.py`, `backend/tests/integration/mcp/test_openapi_export_stable.py`) + **75** auto-generated в `Frontend/src/sdk/argus-mcp/`.
- Файлов изменено: **5** (`Frontend/package.json`, `Frontend/package-lock.json`, `backend/tests/conftest.py`, `.github/workflows/ci.yml`, `docs/mcp-server.md`).
- Спецификация: **22 paths** (15 tools + 4 resources + 0 templates + 3 prompts) / **65 component schemas** / 68 KB.
- TypeScript SDK: **75 файлов** / 74 KB / 3 service-класса / 60+ моделей; `tsc --noEmit` clean.
- Тесты: 23 (`test_mcp_tools_have_docstrings.py`) + 6 (`test_openapi_export_stable.py`) = **29 PASS**, ноль fix-up'ов на существующие descriptions.
- CI gates: `mcp-openapi-drift` блокирует `build` job; новый job в `needs:` рядом с `lint`, `test-no-docker`, `test-docker-required`, `security`, `npm-audit`.
- Backend code НЕ тронут (`backend/src/mcp/{server,runtime,services,tools,resources,prompts}/` — read-only из `openapi_emitter`); ни один tool YAML / signed manifest не перегенерирован.

### Changed (ARG-034 — Cycle 4: Image-build CI gating + GHCR push + Trivy blocking + branch protection, 2026-04-20)

- **`.github/workflows/sandbox-images.yml::build-images`** переключён с локальной сборки на **build + push в `ghcr.io/<org>/argus-kali-<profile>`** для всех четырёх профилей (`web`, `cloud`, `browser`, `full`). Каждый пуш публикует пару тегов: `:<github.sha>` (immutable, content-addressable) и `:latest` (плавающий dev-тег). Авторизация в GHCR — через `docker/login-action@v3` с auto-provisioned `secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN` и `permissions.packages: write` (никаких PAT). Имя организации приводится к нижнему регистру через POSIX `tr` shell-step, потому что GHCR не принимает капитализированные ссылки.
- **OCI SBOM artefact**. После пуша извлекается `sbom.cdx.json` напрямую из образа через `docker run --rm --entrypoint cat <image>:<sha>`, инлайн-валидируется CycloneDX 1.5 envelope (`bomFormat == "CycloneDX"`, `specVersion == "1.5"`, `components` присутствует), затем прикрепляется к манифесту в GHCR командой `cosign attach sbom --type cyclonedx`. Внешние верификаторы могут забрать SBOM без скачивания multi-GB образа: `cosign download sbom <image>:<sha>`. Тот же файл дублируется в workflow-artifact (`sbom-<profile>-<sha>`, retention 30 дней) как backup, не зависящий от доступности GHCR.
- **Cosign pinned to v2.4.1** (`sigstore/cosign-installer@v3.7.0` + `cosign-release: v2.4.1`). Команда `cosign attach sbom` была удалена в cosign v3.x, поэтому пин остаётся на v2-линии до тех пор, пока ARG-033 не переключит механизм на `cosign attest --predicate <sbom> --type cyclonedx` (работает в обеих версиях).
- **Новый job `trivy-scan`** — **БЛОКИРУЮЩИЙ**, заменяет informational-сканер из Cycle 3. Матрица по тем же четырём профилям, depends_on `build-images`. Использует `aquasecurity/trivy-action@0.28.0` с параметрами: `severity: CRITICAL,HIGH`, `ignore-unfixed: false`, `exit-code: '1'`, `trivyignores: '.trivyignore'`, `format: table`. Любой непогашённый CRITICAL или HIGH (fixed ИЛИ unfixed) теперь fail'ит matrix leg и блокирует merge в `main`. `continue-on-error` снят — никакого fall-through.
- **Новый job `compose-smoke`** — закрывает DoD §19.4 partial. Тянет все 4 sandbox-образа из GHCR по `:<sha>`, выполняет per-image smoke check (`docker run --rm <image> id` подтверждает `uid=65532(argus)`, плюс `cat /usr/share/doc/sbom.cdx.json | head -c 256` подтверждает наличие baked-in SBOM), затем поднимает только data-tier из `infra/docker-compose.yml` (`postgres`, `redis`, `minio`, `minio-init`) через `docker compose up -d`. e2e-тесты — Cycle 6, тут только smoke-загрузка контейнеров. Cleanup через `docker compose down -v` в `if: always()`.
- **`paths-filter`** в `on.push.paths` / `on.pull_request.paths` расширен — добавлены `infra/docker-compose.yml` и `.trivyignore`, чтобы изменения в compose-стеке и в curated allowlist триггерили полный sandbox-images pipeline. Существующие триггеры (`sandbox/images/**`, `infra/scripts/build_images.sh`, `infra/scripts/sign_images.sh`, сам workflow) сохранены.
- **`.trivyignore` (NEW, root-level)**. Curated allowlist для CVE-suppressions, которые блокирующий Trivy-скан имеет право игнорировать. Файл создан **пустым** по спецификации — реальный список CVE рождается на первом боевом прогоне. Каждая будущая запись обязана нести четырёхполевой comment block: CVE-ID, justification (какой пакет, какая фича, почему ARGUS sandbox её не вызывает), owner (`ARG-NNN`), expiry (`expires: YYYY-MM-DD`, 90 дней с даты добавления). Ежеквартальный аудит описан inline в шапке файла + в `docs/sandbox-images.md` §4b.2. Никаких wildcard'ов, никаких severity-blanket'ов, никакого возврата `ignore-unfixed: true`.
- **`infra/scripts/build_images.sh`** — добавлен опциональный флаг `--push`. По умолчанию выключен (legacy local-only behaviour сохранён). При `--push` скрипт после успешной сборки выполняет `docker push <image>:<tag>` и `docker push <image>:latest` для каждого профиля. Защита от случайного пуша: `--push` без `--registry` падает с `ERROR: --push requires --registry` (иначе можно было бы случайно пушить в `docker.io/library/argus-kali-*`). Dry-run-режим теперь корректно печатает и build-, и push-команды (раньше push-блок проглатывался полностью при `--dry-run`). Per-profile failure summary различает `(build failed)` vs `(push failed)` для удобства триажа.
- **`docs/sandbox-images.md`** — три новые секции (§4a CI image build + push to GHCR, §4b Trivy blocking scan policy, §4c Branch protection requirements) общим объёмом ~250 строк. §4a описывает pipeline order (mermaid-style), GHCR permissions/secrets matrix, локальные эквиваленты CI-команд для PowerShell + bash, mechanics OCI SBOM attach, и cosign version pin rationale. §4b фиксирует Trivy parameters (locked), `.trivyignore` curation policy (5 правил), local replay command. §4c содержит explicit list из 16 required status checks для merge в `main`, рекомендуемые branch-protection-настройки (с явными «include administrators», «no force pushes», «no deletions»), 9-step setup checklist для оператора, и break-glass procedure на случай GHCR/Sigstore outage. §5.3 переписан под новый `--push` flag.

### Metrics (ARG-034)

- Workflow jobs: 4 → **6** (+2: `trivy-scan`, `compose-smoke`). `build-images` и `sign-images` остались, но получили GHCR push + cosign-attach + cosign v2.4.1 pin.
- Required status checks для `main`: было ~6 (только `ci.yml` + `hardening-contract`), стало **16** (см. §4c.1 в `docs/sandbox-images.md`). Из них 11 — sandbox-images (`hardening-contract` + 4× `build-images` + 4× `trivy-scan` + `compose-smoke` + `verify-images`-после-ARG-033), 5 — `ci.yml` (`lint`, `test-no-docker`, `test-docker-required`, `security`, `npm-audit`).
- Trivy gating: informational (Cycle 3, `exit-code 0`, `continue-on-error: true`, `ignore-unfixed: true`) → **blocking** (`exit-code 1`, `severity CRITICAL,HIGH`, `ignore-unfixed: false`).
- SBOM distribution: было только workflow-artifact (доступен 30 дней через GH UI) → **OCI artefact в GHCR** (доступен через `cosign download sbom`, retention = lifetime образа) + workflow-artifact как fallback.
- `paths-filter` coverage: 4 → **6 paths** (+`.trivyignore`, `infra/docker-compose.yml`).
- Файлов изменено: 4 (`.github/workflows/sandbox-images.yml`, `infra/scripts/build_images.sh`, `docs/sandbox-images.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`). Файлов создано: 1 (`.trivyignore`). Backend Python — **не тронут** (out of scope).
- Verification on Windows worker: `python -m yaml` syntax check на workflow — clean. Local `trivy` / `actionlint` / `shellcheck` skipped (Windows env), боевая верификация — на следующем PR push в `main`.

### Changed (ARG-033 — Cycle 4: Cosign keyless prod wiring + Rekor + SLSA attestation + verify-images CI gate, 2026-04-20)

- **`infra/scripts/sign_images.sh`** переписан с Cycle 3 dry-run-скелета на **production keyless** Cosign-подпись через **Sigstore Fulcio + Rekor**, с автоматическим OIDC-обменом из GitHub Actions (`id-token: write`). Default-путь: `cosign sign --yes <image>` (без `--key`) + `cosign attest --predicate <SBOM> --type cyclonedx --yes <image>` — Rekor-upload включён по дефолту в cosign v2.x. Нет ни одного long-lived secret в job env: identity берётся из ambient JWT, Fulcio выпускает 10-минутный X.509 с SAN, привязанным к workflow path. `--image <ref>` (повторяемый) и `--sbom <path>` флаги добавлены — CI matrix leg подписывает ровно тот же образ, который `build-images` запушил в GHCR, тем же байтовым SBOM, который прошёл inline CycloneDX-валидацию.
- **Keyed rollback path** сохранён под env var `COSIGN_KEY` — emergency runbook на случай Sigstore degraded. При выставленном `COSIGN_KEY` (и без `--dry-run`) скрипт автодетектит rollback-режим, печатает `WARNING: KEYED ROLLBACK MODE` баннер, форсирует `--tlog-upload=false` (нет identity для Rekor), и подписывает long-lived ключом. Public half (`infra/cosign/cosign.pub`) коммитится для верификации; private — repo secret. Post-incident re-sign в keyless mode + revoke ключа описаны в новом §4e runbook'е.
- **`.github/workflows/sandbox-images.yml::sign-images`** переключён на keyless: `secrets.COSIGN_PRIVATE_KEY` / `secrets.COSIGN_PASSWORD` env vars удалены из job, `permissions.id-token: write` сохранён (теперь это mandatory, не optional). Job теперь делает explicit `docker pull <image>:<sha>` + `docker run --entrypoint cat ... > sbom.cdx.json` ДО вызова скрипта, чтобы подписываемый SBOM был байтово идентичен тому, что вшит в образ при build-images. Скрипт вызывается через `--image <ref> --sbom <path>` форму (не `--profile/--tag`) — explicit-image-override path, добавленный в этом же ARG-033.
- **Новый job `verify-images`** в том же workflow: `needs: [sign-images]`, matrix:4 (`web`, `cloud`, `browser`, `full`), `permissions: { contents: read, packages: read }` (без `id-token` — verify не подписывает). На каждый из 4 профилей запускает `cosign verify <image> --certificate-identity-regexp "^https://github\.com/[^/]+/[^/]+/\.github/workflows/sandbox-images\.yml@refs/heads/.+$" --certificate-oidc-issuer "https://token.actions.githubusercontent.com"` + `cosign verify-attestation <image> --type cyclonedx --certificate-identity-regexp ... --certificate-oidc-issuer ...`. Любая missing signature ИЛИ certificate identity mismatch fail'ит matrix leg → блокирует merge (после добавления verify-images в Required Status Checks).
- **Branch protection** — в `docs/sandbox-images.md §4c.1` `verify-images` уже стоит в списке required checks (с пометкой «added by ARG-033»); pre-cycle-4 этот пункт был помечен как «turn ON the day ARG-033 ships». После этого PR — pinned ON.
- **`docs/sandbox-images.md`** — три новые секции (~+520 LoC): **§4d Cosign keyless signing** (trust chain diagram, sign + verify YAML snippets, local equivalent для PowerShell + bash, permissions matrix sign vs verify), **§4e Rollback to keyed mode** (когда применять, 6-step operator runbook, post-incident re-sign procedure, compatibility matrix keyless vs keyed vs dry-run), **§4f Verifying offline** (offline bundle production: `--output-signature` + `--output-certificate`, air-gapped verify через `--insecure-ignore-tlog=true` (cosign v2 syntax), trust-root distribution caveat для не-cosign verifier'ов). Cycle 3 §4 «Cosign signing (skeleton)» секция оставлена нетронутой как историческая справка.
- **Pinned versions** (без изменений по сравнению с ARG-034): `sigstore/cosign-installer@v3.7.0` + `cosign-release: v2.4.1` — те же версии, что используются в `build-images` для `cosign attach sbom`. `actions/checkout@v4`, `docker/login-action@v3`, `actions/upload-artifact@v4` — все pinned.
- **`sign-dry-run` (PR)** — точечная правка: добавлен `Install Cosign v2` step, чтобы PR-валидация имела реальный cosign на PATH (для будущей smoke-инвокации, а не только парсинга `--dry-run`).

Recommended: на первом PR после merge создать issue `ISS-cycle4-arg033-first-keyless-smoke.md` для финального gate.

### Fixed (ARG-037 — Cycle 4: stale-import cleanup batch + Test* class collision rename + payload SIGNATURES drift guard, 2026-04-20)

- **Restored missing per-scan cost-tracker registry** in `backend/src/llm/cost_tracker.py` (`_tracker_registry`, `get_tracker(scan_id, *, max_cost_usd=None)`, `pop_tracker(scan_id)`). Previous refactor dropped these helpers; `src/llm/facade.py::_record_llm_cost` lazy-imported `get_tracker` inside a broad `try/except Exception:` block, so every LLM call with a `scan_id` silently failed to record cost. Net effect: per-scan budget tracking and `GET /scans/{scan_id}/cost` returned `total_cost_usd: 0` for every scan since the regression. Re-exported the new helpers from `backend/src/llm/__init__.py` for API consistency. Closes **ISS-fix-004-imports**.
- **17 stale `F401` imports removed** across `src/dedup/`, `src/recon/exploitation/`, `src/recon/reporting/`, `src/recon/schemas/`, `src/recon/services/`, and `src/sandbox/parsers/`. Net delta: `-17` lines, no behaviour change. Verified each removal against repo-wide grep — no `__init__.py` re-exports the dropped symbols. `python -m ruff check src --select F401,F811` is now clean. Closes **ISS-fix-006-imports**.
- **Payload SIGNATURES drift investigation** — bisected via the documented plan (snapshot SHA-256 → run targeted payload suites → expand to `pytest tests/unit -q` (6190 passed) → expand to `pytest tests/integration -q` (1548 passed) → re-verify hash). Result: drift is **no longer reproducible** (existing `tmp_path`-based fixtures already protect the production catalog). Added a regression guard at `backend/tests/integration/payloads/test_signatures_no_drift.py` (3 tests: snapshot SHA-256 of SIGNATURES, snapshot SHA-256 of every YAML, idempotency over five sequential `PayloadRegistry.load()` calls). The guard runs under the `requires_docker` marker auto-applied to `tests/integration/payloads/` per `tests/conftest.py::_DOCKER_FORCED_PATH_PREFIXES`. Closes **ISS-payload-signatures-drift**.
- **11 `Test*` class name collisions** across **23 test modules** renamed with file/domain context prefixes — `TestAdapterRegistry` → `TestRecon…` / `TestExploitation…`, `TestApprovalRequest` → `TestExploitation…` / `TestPolicy…`, `TestAssertAllowed` → `TestPreflight…` / `TestScope…`, `TestDeterminism` → `TestJunit…` / `TestReportService…` / `TestSarif…`, `TestFullPipeline` → `TestEnrichment…` / `TestXss…`, `TestHappyPath` → `TestPolicyEngine…` / `TestPreflight…`, `TestImmutability` → `TestReportBundle…` / `TestValidationPlan…`, `TestModels` → `TestOwnership…` / `TestPolicyEngine…`, `TestPurgeExpired` → `TestCorrelator…` / `TestProvisioner…`, `TestRunExploitation` → `TestArgus004…` / `TestArgus005…`, `TestToolRunStatus` → `TestMcpSchemas…` / `TestMcpToolCatalog…`. Each rename was a single-class edit (no test inherited from these classes, no internal references). Verified `pytest --collect-only` runs without warnings; `pytest -k <new-name>` uniquely targets each suite. Closes **ISS-pytest-test-prefix-collisions**.
- **Test relocation** — `backend/tests/test_fix_004_cost_tracking.py` → `backend/tests/unit/llm/test_cost_tracker_registry.py` (proper home, prefixed class names: `TestCostTrackerGet`, `TestCostTrackerPop`, `TestCostTrackerRecord`, `TestCostTrackerFacadeIntegration`). `backend/tests/test_fix_006_recon.py` → deleted (two test classes referenced functions that no longer exist; the third duplicated `tests/test_bkl_va_fallback.py::TestBuildVaFallbackOutputOtherTasks::test_unknown_task_returns_structured_fallback` with weaker assertions).

### Fixed (ARG-038 — Cycle 4: apktool.yaml drift root-cause investigation + read-only catalog session fixture + 5-case regression gate, 2026-04-19)

- **Root-cause investigation для исторического `apktool.yaml` drift симптома** (Cycle 3 ARG-021 / 022 / 027 / 029): по плану из `ai_docs/develop/plans/2026-04-19-argus-finalization-cycle4.md` §3 ARG-038 проведён full bisection — snapshot SHA-256 188 защищённых файлов (`config/{tools,payloads,prompts}/*.yaml + SIGNATURES`), затем full `pytest -q` deterministic run (11 222 passed, 5 pre-existing parser failures unrelated to catalog) + 3× targeted high-risk modules sweep (`tests/unit/sandbox tests/integration/sandbox tests/test_tool_catalog_coverage.py`) + code-search всех `write_text` / `write_bytes` / `open(..., "w")` в `backend/tests/` против catalog paths. Результат: drift **не воспроизводится** в Cycle 4 baseline — все 188 файлов bit-for-bit identical. Все unit/integration fixtures корректно используют `tmp_path` / `tmp_path_factory.mktemp(...)`. Наиболее вероятная Cycle 3 гипотеза: либо stale fixture (удалена в более раннем cleanup pass), либо xdist race (xdist в Cycle 4 отключён), либо AV-induced anomaly. Всё задокументировано в **`ai_docs/develop/issues/ISS-apktool-drift-rootcause.md`** (закрывает investigation).
- **Defence-in-depth `read_only_catalog` session fixture** в `backend/tests/conftest.py` — новый `@pytest.fixture(scope="session", autouse=True)` chmod'ит каждый `*.yaml` + `SIGNATURES` под `backend/config/{tools,payloads,prompts}/` в read-only mode на старте session (POSIX: `0o444` через `stat.S_IRUSR | S_IRGRP | S_IROTH`; Windows: `stat.S_IREAD` → `FILE_ATTRIBUTE_READONLY`) и восстанавливает оригинальный mode на teardown. Любая попытка `open(path, "w")` / `path.write_text(...)` / `path.write_bytes(...)` от теста немедленно валится с `PermissionError`, **превращая молчаливую corruption в fail-fast diagnostic**. Helpers `_iter_catalog_files`, `_make_read_only`, `_restore_mode` — pure-Python, cross-platform, теста не требуют (sanity-check выполнен ad-hoc, удалён). Restore в `try/finally`, warning в stderr (не raise) если файл удалён mid-session.
- **Marker `mutates_catalog`** зарегистрирован в `backend/pyproject.toml` + `backend/pytest.ini` для будущих тестов, которым правомерно нужна mutation production catalog'а. Marker — documentation-only: chmod применяется session-wide unconditionally, поэтому даже marked-тест должен использовать `tmp_path` копию (см. canonical pattern `tests/unit/payloads/conftest.py::signed_payloads_dir` и `tests/unit/sandbox/conftest.py::signed_tools_dir`). На текущий момент **ни один существующий тест** не нуждается в этом marker.
- **Регрессионный gate `backend/tests/test_catalog_immutable_during_pytest.py` (NEW, 5 тест-кейсов)**:
  1. `test_signed_catalog_is_read_only_during_pytest_session` — для каждого защищённого файла во всех трёх каталогах ассертит `mode & stat.S_IWUSR == 0` (cross-platform owner-write bit check).
  2. `test_signed_catalog_dirs_are_populated` — sanity: каталоги не пусты (защита от silent cleanup).
  3. `test_signed_catalog_verifies_after_pytest[tools]` — `subprocess.run([python, -m, scripts.tools_sign, verify, ...])` exit 0.
  4. `test_signed_catalog_verifies_after_pytest[payloads]` — `subprocess.run([python, -m, scripts.payloads_sign, verify, ...])` exit 0.
  5. `test_signed_catalog_verifies_after_pytest[prompts]` — `subprocess.run([python, -m, scripts.prompts_sign, verify, ...])` exit 0.
  Если когда-нибудь test обойдёт fixture (например, через explicit `os.chmod(0o644)` mid-run или через `unlink + write` workaround), gate упадёт с понятной диагностикой включающей mode bits + verify stdout/stderr. Файл добавлен в `_OFFLINE_FILE_NAMES` в `tests/conftest.py` (rationale: file-permission + subprocess-based gate, не нуждается в Postgres / Redis / Docker).
- **Smoke loop 5/5 clean** — пять последовательных `pytest -q --tb=line` runs + триплет verify CLIs после каждого: 5/5 catalog `verify.ok` (157 tools + 23 payloads + 5 prompts = 185 entries × 5 runs = **925 successful verifies**), 188 файлов hash-identical baseline после **всех** прогонов. Single test failure (`tests/integration/sandbox/parsers/test_arg029_dispatch.py::test_registered_count_is_68 — assert 98 == 68`) — pre-existing parser-count assertion в скоупе других worker'ов (sandbox/parsers), к catalog drift отношения не имеет, был в baseline ДО ARG-038 changes.

### Metrics (ARG-038)

- Verification gates: `python -m pytest tests/test_catalog_immutable_during_pytest.py -v` → 5 passed. `python -m ruff check tests/conftest.py tests/test_catalog_immutable_during_pytest.py` → All checks passed. `python -m ruff format --check tests/conftest.py tests/test_catalog_immutable_during_pytest.py` → 2 files already formatted. **Smoke loop 5/5 clean** (5× full pytest + 15× verify across 3 catalogs).

### Added (ARG-029 — Cycle 3 batch 3: per-tool parsers JSON_LINES + Custom + JSON_OBJECT mixed, 2026-04-19)

- **15 new per-tool parsers** wired into `src.sandbox.parsers._DEFAULT_TOOL_PARSERS`:
  - **JSON_LINES (4):** `trufflehog`, `naabu`, `masscan`, `prowler`. `trufflehog` redacts every `Raw` / `RawV2` / `Secret` field through `redact_secret(...)` BEFORE the JSONL sidecar is written; integration test asserts the canonical `***REDACTED({len})***` marker is present and that no `[A-Za-z0-9]{40,}` raw-secret blob survives. `prowler` preserves AWS account IDs in `Resource.Identifier` verbatim — they are pivot data, not secrets — and the integration test pins this so a future blanket-redaction sweep cannot regress it.
  - **Custom (5):** `detect_secrets`, `openapi_scanner`, `graphql_cop`, `postman_newman`, `zap_baseline`. `detect_secrets` preserves the `hashed_secret` SHA-1 fingerprint (cross-scan correlation key) but redacts any cleartext `secret` field that ships with newer plugin builds. `postman_newman` scrubs Bearer / JWT / AWS keys from response previews and routes assertion failures through a `secret > auth > security > generic` keyword priority chain. `zap_baseline` stripps inline HTML from `desc` / `solution` / `evidence` (truncated to `_MAX_DESC_PREVIEW`) so the sidecar stays grep-friendly.
  - **Mixed JSON_OBJECT (6):** `syft`, `cloudsploit`, `hashid`, `hash_analyzer`, `jarm`, `wappalyzer_cli`. `syft` always emits an inventory marker finding (component count + image digest) so a clean SBOM is still discoverable; `hashid` and `hash_analyzer` ONLY persist `stable_hash_12(...)` discriminators — raw hash inputs never reach the sidecar. `jarm` accepts three envelope shapes (top-level array, single object, JSONL stream) and drops all-zero fingerprints (no TLS response). `wappalyzer_cli` accepts the modern `{urls, technologies}` envelope and the legacy `[{url, technologies}]` array.
- **Helper reuse only — zero new helpers added.** Every parser composes `safe_decode`, `safe_load_json`, `safe_load_jsonl`, `redact_secret`, `stable_hash_12`, `MAX_STDOUT_BYTES`, `make_finding_dto`, `SENTINEL_CVSS_VECTOR`, `persist_jsonl_sidecar`, `safe_join_artifact` from `_base.py` / `_jsonl_base.py` / `_text_base.py`. Strict adherence to KISS — no parser owns its own JSON loader.
- **15 unit-test suites** in `tests/unit/sandbox/parsers/test_<tool>_parser.py` (≥6 cases each, 354 cases in aggregate including the integration suite below). Per-module coverage: `cloudsploit` 94 %, `detect_secrets` 95 %, `graphql_cop` 99 %, `hash_analyzer` 94 %, `hashid` 92 %, `jarm` 99 %, `masscan` 91 %, `naabu` 99 %, `openapi_scanner` 95 %, `postman_newman` 99 %, `prowler` 94 %, `syft` 91 %, `trufflehog` 92 %, `wappalyzer_cli` 97 %, `zap_baseline` 96 %. Every module ≥ 90 %.
- **15 realistic fixtures** in `tests/fixtures/sandbox_outputs/<tool>/sample.txt` consumed by both unit + integration suites. Each fixture mirrors the real tool's output shape (e.g. `prowler` array of CIS-GCP findings, `cloudsploit` resource buckets, `syft` CycloneDX 1.5 SBOM, `zap_baseline` `<site>/<alerts>/<instances>` tree).
- **Integration suite `tests/integration/sandbox/parsers/test_arg029_dispatch.py`** — 60 cases covering registration, dispatch through `dispatch_parse(...)`, dedicated sidecar generation, unique-sidecar-filename / cross-tool-isolation invariants, deterministic re-runs, and the three CRITICAL security gates: (a) `trufflehog` redacts every long alphanumeric secret to `***REDACTED({len})***`, (b) `hashid` / `hash_analyzer` never persist raw hash bytes, (c) `prowler` preserves AWS account IDs in `Resource.Identifier`. Skips the `binary_blob` family by design (handled upstream in `ShellToolAdapter`).
- **`tests/test_tool_catalog_coverage.py` ratchet bumped:** parser-coverage gate raised from `mapped=53 / heartbeat=104` (post-ARG-022) to `mapped=68 / heartbeat=89`. New `test_arg029_parsers_have_first_class_handlers` test pins the 15 ARG-029 tool IDs to `mapped` so a future regression cannot silently drop them back to the heartbeat fallback.

### Changed (ARG-029)

- `src/sandbox/parsers/__init__.py` — `_DEFAULT_TOOL_PARSERS` extended with the 15 new entries; module docstring updated to mention the new batch.
- `src/sandbox/parsers/postman_newman_parser.py` — `_redact_token_payload` final fallback now coerces `redact_secret(...)` `None` returns to `<REDACTED-TOKEN>` so the function's `str | None` contract is preserved (mypy strict).
- `tests/unit/sandbox/parsers/test_prowler_parser.py` / `test_syft_parser.py` / `test_trufflehog_parser.py` — removed unused `ConfidenceLevel` import and dead `findings = ...` assignments flagged by ruff `F401` / `F841`.

### Added (ARG-026 — Cycle 3: Multi-stage Dockerfiles + SBOM + Cosign skeleton, 2026-04-19)

- **Four production-ready sandbox images** in `sandbox/images/argus-kali-{web,cloud,browser,full}/Dockerfile`. Each replaces the Cycle 2 header-only stub with a real multi-stage `kalilinux/kali-rolling:2026.1` build: a `builder` stage with Go 1.22 + Python 3.12 + Node 22 + apt build deps, and a slim runtime stage that COPYs only the user-prefix install trees from the builder. Every image bakes pinned tool versions (16 Go binaries + 14 PyPI wheels + 2 npm packages + wpscan ruby gem on `web`; 7 Go + 10 PyPI + 3 release tarballs + cloudsploit npm on `cloud`; playwright + pyppeteer + puppeteer + retire.js on `browser`; superset on `full` with relaxed apt pinning by spec). Final stage runs as `USER 65532` with `WORKDIR /home/argus`, ships the canonical OCI labels (`org.opencontainers.image.{title,description,source,version,licenses}`) plus ARGUS-specific `argus.image.{profile,cycle}` and `argus.sbom.path` labels, and exits with a healthcheck wired to a shared script. The `browser` image explicitly removes `/usr/lib/chromium/chrome-sandbox` + `chrome_crashpad_handler-suid` to maintain the no-SUID contract — Chromium runs in `--no-sandbox` under the k8s seccomp / read-only-fs / runAsNonRoot triple defence.
- **Two shared helpers** in `sandbox/images/_shared/`:
  - `healthcheck.sh` (24 LoC) — minimal `echo ok && exit 0` probe. Cycle 4 will replace it with a real readiness check tied to the supervisor sidecar; keeping it as a shared file lets us evolve the probe without touching every Dockerfile.
  - `generate_sbom.sh` (104 LoC) — CycloneDX 1.5 JSON emitter. Prefers `syft` when present (cloud + full), falls back to a `dpkg-query`-driven envelope built with raw `printf` (no Python dep, no jq dep, no network). Output lands at `/usr/share/doc/sbom.cdx.json` and is referenced by the `argus.sbom.path` label.
- **Build + sign helpers** in `infra/scripts/`:
  - `build_images.sh` — local helper that iterates the 4 profiles, takes `--profile {web,cloud,browser,full,all}` + `--tag <ver>` + `--registry <prefix>` + `--no-cache` + `--dry-run`, double-tags every build with the explicit version + `:latest`, and surfaces a per-profile failure summary.
  - `sign_images.sh` — Cosign signing pipeline skeleton. Defaults to dry-run (prints the `cosign sign` + `cosign attest --type cyclonedx` invocations without requiring a key); switches to real signing when `COSIGN_KEY` is set (`--tlog-upload=false`, no Rekor / Fulcio yet — Cycle 5 swap). Emits a `cosign-bundle.json` artifact listing every signed `(image, timestamp)` pair.
- **CI workflow** at `.github/workflows/sandbox-images.yml` — four jobs: (1) `hardening-contract` (Python static analysis of the Dockerfiles, runs on every PR + push), (2) `build-images` (matrix over `[web, cloud, browser, full]`, builds via `build_images.sh`, extracts SBOM with `docker run --entrypoint cat`, validates the CycloneDX envelope inline with a 9-line Python check, uploads SBOM as artifact, runs informational Trivy scan), (3) `sign-images` (only on push to `main`, runs `sign_images.sh` with `COSIGN_PRIVATE_KEY` + `COSIGN_PASSWORD` secrets, falls back to dry-run if either is unset), (4) `sign-dry-run` (PRs only, validates the script wires up end-to-end without secrets).
- **Hardening contract test** at `backend/tests/integration/sandbox/test_image_security_contract.py` — 65 static-analysis assertions, no Docker daemon required, runs in <1 s. Bespoke regex-based Dockerfile parser (`_strip_comments_and_continuations` joins backslash-continuations, `_parse_stages` keys directives by FROM boundaries, `_final_stage` returns the runtime stage). Test classes:
  - `TestStructure` — file existence, multi-stage pattern (≥1 builder + ≥1 final non-builder stage).
  - `TestUserDirective` — `USER 65532` in final stage AND `useradd --uid 65532` + `groupadd --gid 65532` in any stage.
  - `TestHealthcheck` — `HEALTHCHECK` directive in final stage, invokes `/usr/local/bin/healthcheck.sh`.
  - `TestLabels` — required OCI labels present, required ARGUS labels present, `argus.image.profile` matches the parent directory name, `argus.image.cycle == "ARG-026"`, `argus.sbom.path == "/usr/share/doc/sbom.cdx.json"`.
  - `TestSbomGeneration` — `generate_sbom.sh` invoked at build time, targets the canonical SBOM path.
  - `TestNoSuidIntroduction` — six regex patterns reject `chmod +s`, `chmod u+s`, `chmod g+s`, `chmod ug+s`, `chmod a+s`, AND `chmod 0?[2467][0-7]{3}` (catches octal SUID introductions like `chmod 4755`).
  - `TestSharedHelpers` — both `_shared/*.sh` files exist with shebangs + the required content markers (CycloneDX in the SBOM helper, `exit 0` in the healthcheck), and every Dockerfile COPYs them.
  - `TestProfileSpecificContracts` — browser image documents Chromium SUID removal, cloud image ships syft, full image is a true superset (contains nuclei + trivy + chromium signature tools).
  - `TestBaseImagePin` — every stage is built from `kalilinux/kali-rolling:<pin>` (not `:latest`); reproducibility guard.
- **Documentation** at `docs/sandbox-images.md` — image profile matrix (4 profiles × tools count + backlog references), per-image pinned-version table, hardening-contract reference (16 invariants × where each is enforced), runtime k8s securityContext block, SBOM regen recipe (in-image extraction + forced regeneration + CI validation snippet), Cosign signing recipe (PR dry-run + local real signing + CI secrets), local build workflow recipes, "adding a new profile" 5-step procedure, known follow-ups list.
- **Follow-up issue** at `ai_docs/develop/issues/ISS-cycle3-tool-yaml-version-field.md` — ARG-026 brief expected per-tool YAMLs to carry a `version:` field; they don't, and `ToolDescriptor` doesn't expose one. The pinned versions therefore live exclusively in the Dockerfiles + `docs/sandbox-images.md` for Cycle 3. Cycle 4 will backfill the `version:` field, add a `ToolDescriptor.version` Pydantic field, and add a sandbox-driver pre-flight that warns on `(catalog version vs. argus.image.version)` mismatch.

### Metrics (ARG-026)

- Sandbox images shipped: stub (4) → **production-ready (4)**, all 4 satisfy the full hardening contract.
- Hardening contract assertions: **65 / 65 PASS** (`tests/integration/sandbox/test_image_security_contract.py`, `pytest -q` 0.98 s).
- Sandbox integration regression: **1407 / 1407 PASS** (`tests/integration/sandbox`, excluding the new file, 70.43 s).
- Total sandbox test surface: **1472 / 1472 PASS**.
- `ruff check` + `ruff format --check` on the new test file — clean.
- Pinned tool versions baked into Dockerfiles: web 16 Go + 14 Py + 2 npm + 1 ruby gem; cloud 7 Go + 10 Py + 3 release tarballs + 1 npm; browser 2 Py + 2 npm; full superset (16 Go + 8 Py).
- CI workflow jobs: 4 (`hardening-contract`, `build-images` matrix-of-4, `sign-images`, `sign-dry-run`).
- Dockerfile LoC total (4 files): **822 lines** (web 240 + cloud 175 + browser 172 + full 194 + shared 24 + 104).
- `docker build` smoke test: **deferred** to Cycle 5 capstone (no Docker daemon available in the local dev environment; CI exercises the real build via the `build-images` matrix on every PR).

### Added (ARG-025 — Cycle 3: Asgard tier + replay_command_sanitizer, 2026-04-19)

- **`backend/src/reports/replay_command_sanitizer.py`** — new pure-function module that scrubs every embedded reproducer `argv` before it leaves the pipeline. Single public entry point `sanitize_replay_command(argv: list[str], context: SanitizeContext) -> list[str]` plus a frozen Pydantic `SanitizeContext(target, endpoints, canaries)`. Pipeline (run in order, all pure helpers): (1) drop destructive flags by exact-equality (`--rm`, `-rf`, `-fr`, `--force`, `--no-confirm`, `--yes`, `--skip-checks`, `--insecure`, `--ignore-cert`, `--ignore-ssl-errors`, `--ignore-tls-errors`, `--no-check-certificate`, `--allow-insecure-localhost`); (2) redact password-flag values across both split-token (`--password VALUE`) and inline-`=` / inline-`:` (`-p=VALUE`, `--token:VALUE`) forms; (3) per-token regex sweep over `_SECRET_PATTERNS` with canary-aware replacement; (4) reverse-shell scrub (`/dev/tcp/...`, `nc -e`, `import socket`, `pty.spawn`, `use Socket`, `| sh`, `IEX (`, `Invoke-Expression`, `DownloadString(`, `mkfifo`); (5) target / endpoint substitution (`{ASSET}` / `{ENDPOINT}`). All steps honour the operator's canary list (any token containing a canary substring is passed through verbatim — OAST / blind-XSS markers stay legible). Type-strict (raises `TypeError` for non-`list[str]` inputs and non-`SanitizeContext` context). Idempotent: re-running on already-sanitised output is a byte-perfect no-op.
- **`backend/src/reports/asgard_tier_renderer.py`** — Asgard-specific section assembler that builds an immutable `AsgardSectionAssembly` Pydantic model (`findings`, `remediation`, `reproducer_commands`, `timeline`, `evidence`, `screenshots`, `owasp_rollup`). Each block is a frozen Pydantic submodel so the assembly can be hashed, cached, and serialised deterministically. Findings ordered severity → CVSS desc → title → CWE; remediation pulled from per-finding metadata with a program-level fallback; reproducers extracted from both `proof_of_concept.replay_command` (list form) and `proof_of_concept.reproducer` (string form); timeline normalised; evidence + screenshots passed through an optional `presigner: Callable[[str], str | None]` callback. When `presigner` is omitted the assembly emits `presigned_url=None` and the report still renders cleanly with the bare object key.
- **Tier classifier extended for Asgard (`tier_classifier.py`):** new `_project_asgard` branch that keeps the full finding set + remediation + sanitised reproducers + timeline + phase outputs + evidence + screenshots + AI insights, but still strips raw artefact dumps and HIBP password rows (those remain Valhalla-only). `classify_for_tier` now accepts an optional `sanitize_context` kwarg that is threaded all the way through `_project_asgard` → `_sanitise_finding` → `sanitize_replay_command`, so operator-supplied canaries / endpoints / asset URLs influence the redaction. Backwards-compatible: callers that omit `sanitize_context` get a minimal context built from `data.target`.
- **`ReportService.render_bundle` Asgard branch** — when `tier == ReportTier.ASGARD` the service builds `AsgardSectionAssembly` via `assemble_asgard_sections(...)` and splices it into the Jinja context as `asgard_report`. The existing `generators.generate_html` / `generate_pdf` are wired through unchanged (no legacy rewrite per the architecture invariant); `generate_json` was extended to merge the `asgard_report` blob into the JSON payload (mirrors the existing Valhalla wiring); `generate_csv` was hardened to set `lineterminator="\n"` so snapshots are byte-stable across Windows / Linux.
- **HTML/PDF wiring** preserved through the legacy `generators.py` surface; the Asgard branch hands the projected `ReportData` + `asgard_report` context to the same Jinja template renderer, then to WeasyPrint for PDF (skip-on-missing native libs).
- **`backend/tests/unit/reports/test_replay_command_sanitizer.py`** — 38 unit cases covering every secret class (Bearer / JWT / AWS key + secret / GitHub PAT family / GitLab PAT / Slack tokens / Stripe / Twilio / GCP / Azure / SendGrid / Mailgun / generic kv / password kv / NT-LM pair / standalone empty-LM / private keys), destructive-flag stripping, reverse-shell scrubs, target / endpoint substitution, canary preservation, idempotency, and `TypeError` propagation for malformed inputs.
- **`backend/tests/unit/reports/test_asgard_tier_renderer.py`** — 21 unit cases covering severity/CVSS ordering, remediation block assembly, reproducer extraction (both shapes), sanitiser application, timeline ordering, evidence presigning (with and without callback), screenshot dedup, OWASP A01–A10 rollup, and round-trip determinism.
- **`backend/tests/integration/reports/test_asgard_tier_all_formats.py`** — integration suite parametrised over every `ReportFormat` (HTML, PDF, JSON, CSV, SARIF, JUnit). Each format: builds the bundle end-to-end, asserts SHA-256 integrity, cross-run byte identity, presence of the sanitised reproducer (HTML / JSON / CSV / JUnit — SARIF intentionally omits raw PoC bodies), and a regex sweep against the bundle bytes for `Bearer ey…` / `AKIA…` / `password=…` / `nc -e` / `--rm` leaks. Snapshot tests cover JSON / CSV / SARIF / JUnit / HTML byte-equality (HTML is pure Jinja → byte-stable) plus a structural PDF assertion (page count ≥ 1, magic header, `Asgard` text, `[REDACTED-BEARER]` placeholder visible).
- **`backend/tests/security/test_report_no_secret_leak.py`** — security-auditor gate: 53-pattern catalogue (≥50 per spec) covering the full secret taxonomy (Bearer / JWT / cookies / AWS / GCP / Azure / GitHub / GitLab / Slack / Stripe / Twilio / SendGrid / Mailgun / generic kv / password flags / NT-LM / private keys / 12 reverse-shell variants). Two sweeps per pattern: (1) direct `sanitize_replay_command` invocation, (2) end-to-end `ReportService.render_bundle` for the Asgard tier × HTML / JSON / CSV / SARIF / JUnit. Each pattern carries an explicit `needle` substring whose presence in the output is proof of leak — no fuzzy / heuristic matching. Plus `test_canary_token_is_preserved`, `test_destructive_flags_stripped_end_to_end`, and `test_defence_regexes_catch_nothing_in_clean_asgard_output` as cross-cutting invariants.
- **Snapshots** in `backend/tests/snapshots/reports/asgard_canonical.{html,json,csv,sarif,xml}` lock the byte-exact rendered output for the canonical Asgard fixture. Refresh recipe documented in `docs/report-service.md`.
- **`docs/report-service.md`** — new "ARG-025 — Asgard tier" section: tier diff table (Midgard → Asgard delta), full sanitiser contract (NIST SP 800-204D §5.1.4 / OWASP ASVS L2 §V8), pattern catalogue at-a-glance, rendering API recipe with `presigner`, snapshot regen recipe, and security-gate invariants.

### Metrics (ARG-025)

- New modules: `replay_command_sanitizer.py` (533 LoC), `asgard_tier_renderer.py` (~440 LoC); modifications to `tier_classifier.py`, `report_service.py`, `generators.py`.
- Sanitiser pattern catalogue: **17 secret regexes** + **13 reverse-shell regexes** + **13 destructive flags** + **9 password / token flag aliases**.
- Test surface: **38 sanitiser unit cases**, **21 Asgard renderer unit cases**, **24 integration cases** (1 PDF skipped on hosts without WeasyPrint), **53-pattern × 5-format security sweep = 265 + 18 cross-cutting cases**. Total new tests ≈ **394** (all green).
- Security-gate coverage: ≥50 distinct secret / destructive patterns (spec: ≥50). Zero raw secret bytes survive end-to-end across HTML / JSON / CSV / SARIF / JUnit.
- Regression: `tests/integration/reports/` **57 passed, 5 skipped** (Midgard + Asgard suites both green); `tests/test_argus009_reports.py` + `tests/test_bkl_reports.py` unchanged.
- Architecture invariants honoured: sanitiser is a separate module (not inline in any reports/* renderer); legacy `generators.py` HTML/PDF wrapped through `ReportService` (no rewrite); backward compat preserved for ARG-024 Midgard tests; `ReportBundle.sha256` integrity untouched; tier rules remain pure functions.

### Added (ARG-028 — Cycle 3: SQLite test pool fix + pytest marker discipline, 2026-04-19)

- **Dialect-aware SQLAlchemy pool** in `backend/src/db/session.py`. New helpers `_is_sqlite_url`, `_engine_kwargs_for`, and `_build_engine` return `StaticPool` (with `connect_args={"check_same_thread": False}`) for `sqlite*` DSNs and the previous `QueuePool` knobs (`pool_pre_ping=True`, `pool_size=5`, `max_overflow=10`) for everything else. Both the module-level `engine` and `create_task_engine_and_session()` go through the same dispatch, so Celery tasks inherit the same dialect-correct pool. Production behaviour against Postgres is byte-identical; the test harness can now point `DATABASE_URL` at `sqlite+aiosqlite:///:memory:` without the `Invalid argument(s) 'pool_size','max_overflow' sent to create_engine()` `TypeError` that broke ~3170 tests at collection time in Cycle 2 capstone.
- **Auto-classifier in `backend/tests/conftest.py`** — `pytest_collection_modifyitems` walks every collected item and adds `requires_postgres` / `requires_redis` / `requires_oast` / `requires_docker` markers based on (1) explicit offline allowlist (`tests/unit/`, `tests/integration/sandbox/`, `tests/schemas/`, `tests/recon/`, `tests/reports/`, `tests/storage/`, `tests/test_tool_catalog_coverage.py`), (2) docker-forced path prefixes (all `tests/integration/` except `sandbox/`), (3) root-level `tests/test_*.py` legacy bucket (autouse `override_auth(app)` chain pulls in `main.app`), (4) `client` fixture detection, and (5) module-content regex scan for hard-coded `localhost:5432` / `redis://` / `apply_async(` / `interactsh-server` / `RealOASTListener` / `OAST_LISTENER_URL`. Per-file content scans are memoised so the 12k-item collection does not re-read 250 files.
- **Markers registered** in `backend/pytest.ini` (authoritative for pytest) and mirrored in `backend/pyproject.toml` (for IDE / tool discovery): `requires_postgres`, `requires_redis`, `requires_oast`, `requires_docker`, plus the previously-undeclared `weasyprint_pdf` and `no_auth_override`. Default `addopts` carries `-m "not requires_docker"` so the dev workflow (`python -m pytest -q`) skips the Docker-bound suite.
- **CI split** in `.github/workflows/ci.yml`. The single `test` job became two parallel jobs: `test-no-docker` (no service containers, runs the developer's default `pytest tests --tb=short`, `DATABASE_URL=sqlite+aiosqlite:///:memory:`) and `test-docker-required` (Postgres 15 + pgvector + Redis 7 service containers, runs Alembic migrations, then `pytest tests -m "requires_docker" --tb=short -o "addopts="`). `build` depends on both.
- **Triage report** at `ai_docs/develop/issues/ISS-cycle3-test-categorization.md` — full breakdown of why the original ~3170 estimate became ~2906 after the session.py fix landed (250 collection-time errors went away, 1572-item `tests/test_tool_catalog_coverage.py` is offline by spec).
- **Developer + CI guide** at `docs/testing-strategy.md` — marker semantics, run recipes (`pytest -q`, `pytest -m requires_docker -o "addopts="`), troubleshooting matrix, pool-architecture rationale.
- **Unit suite for the pool helpers** at `backend/tests/unit/db/test_session_pool.py` — 14 cases covering: parametrised SQLite-DSN detection across `sqlite://`, `sqlite+aiosqlite://`, `sqlite+pysqlite://`, file-backed and in-memory variants; rejection of `postgresql://`, `postgresql+asyncpg://`, `postgresql+psycopg2://`, `mysql://`; `_engine_kwargs_for` shape per dialect; `_build_engine` returning a `StaticPool` engine for SQLite and an `AsyncAdaptedQueuePool` (size 5) engine for Postgres; and `create_task_engine_and_session()` mirroring the same dispatch via `monkeypatch`.

### Metrics (ARG-028)

- Total tests collected (no marker filter): **12 184**.
- Default-mode (`-m "not requires_docker"`): **9 278** items collected, **0 connection-refused**.
- `requires_docker`: **2 906** items across 232 files; `requires_postgres` 2 906, `requires_redis` 2 896, `requires_oast` 11.
- Offline smoke runs all green: `tests/unit` **5 814 / 5 814 PASS**, `tests/schemas + tests/recon + tests/reports + tests/storage` **485 / 485 PASS**, `tests/test_tool_catalog_coverage.py` **1 572 / 1 572 PASS**, `tests/integration/sandbox` **1 407 / 1 407 PASS**, `tests/unit/db/test_session_pool.py` **14 / 14 PASS**.
- `mypy --strict src/db/session.py` — clean. `mypy --strict tests/conftest.py` — only the four pre-existing fixture-typing errors remain (`app`, `override_auth`, `_mock_auth`, `client`); the ARG-028 hook code is annotated end-to-end and adds zero new errors.
- `ruff check` and `ruff format --check` on `tests/conftest.py`, `src/db/session.py`, `tests/unit/db/test_session_pool.py` — clean.

### Added (ARG-027 — Cycle 3: NetworkPolicy override consumption + cloud-{gcp,azure} templates, 2026-04-19)

- **Three new NetworkPolicy templates** (`cloud-aws`, `cloud-gcp`, `cloud-azure`) seeded into `NETWORK_POLICY_NAMES` (8 → 11 total). Each template opens TCP/443 against `0.0.0.0/0` minus the private + IMDS deny block (`10/8`, `172.16/12`, `192.168/16`, `169.254.169.254/32`, `169.254/16`) and ships a documentation-only FQDN allow-list (`*.amazonaws.com`, `*.googleapis.com`, `*.azure.com`, etc.) surfaced via the `argus.io/egress-fqdns` annotation for downstream Cilium / Calico FQDN policies.
- **`NetworkPolicyTemplate` model gained two fields:** `egress_except_cidrs` (per-template `ipBlock.except` list) and `egress_allowed_fqdns` (annotation-only FQDN intent). Both are validated by Pydantic and immutable (`frozen=True`).
- **Per-tool override consumption (closes ARG-019 H2 reviewer gap):** `NetworkPolicyRef.dns_resolvers` (replace) and `NetworkPolicyRef.egress_allowlist` (union) are now consumed end-to-end by `render_networkpolicy_manifest` and `KubernetesSandboxAdapter.build_networkpolicy_manifest`. Previously the fields were dead config.
- **Override validation (`_validated_dns_overrides` / `_validated_egress_overrides`):** rejects entries that overlap the private + IMDS deny block, FQDN-shaped DNS resolvers (NetworkPolicy v1 ipBlock cannot match on names), garbage CIDRs, and empty / non-string entries. Emits `ValueError` at render time, translated to `SandboxConfigError` by the adapter so the API surface gets a stable exception type.
- **Defence-in-depth invariant:** every wildcard `ipBlock` peer (`0.0.0.0/0` or IPv6 `::/0`) automatically carries the private + IMDS deny list as `ipBlock.except`. This applies to template-static peers, override peers, and any future code path that reaches `_build_ip_block_peer` — strictly safer than the pre-ARG-027 behaviour which emitted naked wildcards without exceptions.
- **`build_networkpolicy_for_job` helper in `src/sandbox/manifest.py`:** bridges `NetworkPolicyRef` → `render_networkpolicy_manifest`, with a name-consistency assertion that catches mis-routed template lookups upstream. Exported from `src.sandbox` package.
- **Unit tests (+20 cases):** `tests/unit/sandbox/test_network_policies.py` extended for the three cloud templates, override replacement vs. union semantics, dedup, FQDN annotation surfacing, and the full negative-validation matrix (private CIDRs, IMDS literal, garbage strings, FQDN-as-DNS-resolver).
- **Integration tests:** new `tests/integration/sandbox/test_network_policy_overrides.py` (20 cases) drives the full `KubernetesSandboxAdapter.build_networkpolicy_manifest` → `apply_networkpolicy` → DRY_RUN YAML round-trip, asserting overrides survive serialisation, garbage is rejected as `SandboxConfigError`, and `cloud-gcp` / `cloud-azure` render with the correct FQDN annotations.
- **Docs:** `docs/network-policies.md` documents all 11 templates (egress shape, ports, intent), the override semantics, the defence-in-depth invariants, and the renderer call graph.

### Changed (ARG-027)

- `_build_ip_block_peer` now filters `egress_except_cidrs` against each peer's `cidr` so only valid subnets are emitted (Kubernetes `ipBlock.except` MUST be a subnet of `cidr` — silently dropping mismatches keeps narrow override peers spec-compliant while letting the cloud templates declare a single deny-list).
- `KubernetesSandboxAdapter.build_networkpolicy_manifest` delegates to `manifest.build_networkpolicy_for_job` and translates render-time `ValueError`s into `SandboxConfigError` (closed-taxonomy `failure_reason: config`).

### Metrics (ARG-027)

- NetworkPolicy templates: 8 → **11** (+3).
- Sandbox + coverage test surface: **7262 / 7262 PASS** (`tests/unit/sandbox + tests/integration/sandbox + tests/test_tool_catalog_coverage.py`); +126 PASS in the focused override suite (`tests/unit/sandbox/test_network_policies.py` + `tests/integration/sandbox/test_network_policy_overrides.py`).
- `mypy --strict src/sandbox/{network_policies,manifest,k8s_adapter}.py` — clean. `mypy --strict` on the two new test files — clean.
- `ruff check + format` on all modified files — clean.
- Override fields previously dead (ARG-019 H2): **0 → 100 % consumed** (verified by integration tests + DRY_RUN YAML round-trip).

### Added (ARG-021 — Cycle 3 batch 1: per-tool parsers JSON_OBJECT IaC/SAST/Cloud, 2026-04-19)

- **10 new per-tool parsers** wired into `src.sandbox.parsers._DEFAULT_TOOL_PARSERS` (`bandit`, `gitleaks`, `kube_bench`, `checkov`, `kics`, `terrascan`, `tfsec`, `dockle`, `mobsf_api`, `grype`). Each is a pure `(stdout, stderr, artifacts_dir, tool_id) -> list[FindingDTO]` function with deterministic dedup, severity / confidence / category mapping, CWE extraction, and tool-tagged JSONL evidence sidecar.
- **Shared parser helpers in `src/sandbox/parsers/_base.py`:** `redact_secret(...)` (configurable head/tail mask, `***REDACTED({len})***` marker) and `stable_hash_12(...)` (deterministic dedup discriminator) — used by every gitleaks / mobsf-secrets path so raw cleartext never reaches sidecars.
- **Integration suite `tests/integration/sandbox/parsers/test_arg021_dispatch.py`:** 35 cases covering registration, dispatch, sidecar isolation, gitleaks redaction guardrail, cross-routing inertness, multi-tool one-`/out` isolation, and deterministic re-runs.
- **Per-parser unit suites:** 144 new tests across 10 files in `tests/unit/sandbox/parsers/test_<tool>_parser.py` (≥10 cases each).

### Changed (ARG-021)

- `tests/integration/sandbox/parsers/test_trivy_semgrep_dispatch.py` — `DEFERRED_ARG018_TOOL_IDS` trimmed to remove the 10 newly-wired tools.

### Added (ARG-022 — Cycle 3 batch 2: per-tool parsers TEXT_LINES Network/Auth/Post-exploit, 2026-04-19)

- **10 new per-tool parsers** wired into `src.sandbox.parsers._DEFAULT_TOOL_PARSERS` (`impacket_secretsdump`, `evil_winrm`, `kerbrute`, `bloodhound_python`, `snmpwalk`, `ldapsearch`, `smbclient` (registers `smbclient_check`), `smbmap`, `enum4linux_ng`, `rpcclient_enum`). Each is a pure `(stdout, stderr, artifacts_dir, tool_id) -> list[FindingDTO]` function with deterministic dedup, severity / confidence / category mapping, CWE / OWASP-WSTG anchoring, and tool-tagged JSONL evidence sidecar.
- **Shared text-line helpers in `src/sandbox/parsers/_text_base.py`:** `parse_kv_lines(...)`, `extract_regex_findings(...)`, `redact_hash_string(...)`, `redact_hashes_in_evidence(...)`. Single auditable surface for the LM/NT/SHA-1/SHA-256/AES/Kerberos blob redaction regexes used by every credential-handling parser. 100 % unit-test coverage (18 cases).
- **CRITICAL — `impacket_secretsdump` hash redaction** enforced by a three-layer guardrail: (1) helper-level unit tests on `redact_hash_string`, (2) parser-level unit test asserting raw hashes never reach `FindingDTO.evidence`, and (3) integration test `test_impacket_secretsdump_redacts_hashes_in_sidecar` in `tests/integration/sandbox/parsers/test_arg022_dispatch.py` that runs the canonical NTDS.dit fixture through `dispatch_parse` and asserts both `\b[a-fA-F0-9]{32}:[a-fA-F0-9]{32}\b` (LM:NT pair) **and** `\b[a-fA-F0-9]{32,}\b` (lone ≥ 32-hex blob — catches SHA-1 / SHA-256 / AES key leakage) return **0 hits** on the resulting JSONL sidecar, plus a positive assertion that the canonical `[REDACTED-NT-HASH]` marker IS present.
- **`snmpwalk` default-community detection** (CWE-256) routes `community public` / `community private` lines to a dedicated high-severity finding instead of the `info`-bucket of generic sys*-disclosure findings.
- **`ldapsearch` privileged-group detection** raises severity for memberships in `Domain Admins` / `Enterprise Admins` / `Schema Admins` / similar; hash-shaped LDIF attribute values (e.g. `unicodePwd`) routed through `redact_hash_string`.
- **Integration suite `tests/integration/sandbox/parsers/test_arg022_dispatch.py`:** 53 cases covering registration sanity, dispatch routing per tool, sidecar isolation, the impacket hash-redaction guardrail, 7-pair cross-routing inertness (`kerbrute↔smbmap`, `smbmap↔kerbrute`, `ldapsearch↔snmpwalk`, `snmpwalk↔ldapsearch`, `rpcclient_enum↔smbclient`, `evil_winrm↔bloodhound_python`, `impacket_secretsdump↔evil_winrm`), 10 × determinism pairs, multi-tool one-`/out` isolation, and a hard `test_registered_count_is_53` ratchet.
- **Per-parser unit suites:** 122 new tests across 11 files (10 parsers + helper) in `tests/unit/sandbox/parsers/test_<tool>_parser.py` (≥ 6 cases each, ≥ 10 in practice for most parsers).
- **10 realistic fixtures** under `backend/tests/fixtures/sandbox_outputs/<tool>/sample.txt` (≥ 10 lines of upstream output each, including a 5-principal NTDS.dit dump + machine account + cleartext + AES key + Kerberos blob for the impacket fixture).

### Changed (ARG-022)

- `tests/test_tool_catalog_coverage.py` — added pinned constants `MAPPED_PARSER_COUNT = 53` and `HEARTBEAT_PARSER_COUNT = 104`, plus a new ratchet test `test_parser_coverage_counts_match_arg022_ratchet` so any drop in mapped parsers (or rise in mapped without a 1-for-1 drop in heartbeat) fails CI loudly.

## ARGUS Active Pentest Engine v1 — Cycle 4 (ARG-031..ARG-040) — 2026-04-20

Сводный rollup цикла 4. Подробности по каждой задаче — в `Cycle 4` секциях выше (`Added (ARG-031)` … `Added (ARG-040)`) и в worker-отчётах `ai_docs/develop/reports/2026-04-19-arg-03*-report.md`. Финальный sign-off отчёт — `ai_docs/develop/reports/2026-04-19-argus-finalization-cycle4.md`.

### Summary

Цикл 4 закрыл оба ключевых reporting-долга и три структурных направления, которые блокировали production rollout: (1) **ReportService Tier 3 (Valhalla)** замкнул матрицу 12 / 18 → **18 / 18** ячеек с branded PDF templates (WeasyPrint primary + LaTeX Phase-1 fallback + deterministic watermark) для всех трёх tier'ов; (2) **per-tool парсеры batch 4** добавили 30 новых модулей (mapped 68 → **98**, heartbeat 89 → **59**, catalog coverage 43.3 % → **62.4 %**) с критическим browser-tier breakthrough (0 % → 100 % для playwright/puppeteer/chrome_csp_probe/webanalyze/gowitness/whatweb) и комплексной credential-redaction infrastructure (cleartext password / NTLM `LM:NT` / NTLMv1-2 hash blob / SAM dump — четыре уровня defence-in-depth); (3) **supply-chain в production**: GHCR push live (`ghcr.io/<org>/argus-kali-{web,cloud,browser,full}:<sha>` + `:latest`), Cosign **keyless signing** через Sigstore Fulcio + Rekor + GH OIDC (zero long-lived secrets в job env), `verify-images` blocking CI gate (matrix 4 / 4), Trivy переключён с informational → **blocking** (`severity: CRITICAL,HIGH`, `ignore-unfixed: false`), 16 required status checks для merge в `main`; (4) **MCP capability surface formalisation**: webhook integrations (Slack incoming-webhook + Linear GraphQL + Jira REST v3) feature-gated через `MCP_NOTIFICATIONS_ENABLED` с per-(adapter × tenant) circuit breaker + retry с exponential jittered backoff, token-bucket rate limiter (`InMemory` + `RedisTokenBucket` с atomic Lua-script EVALSHA) с dual budget enforcement (per-client × per-tenant), OpenAPI 3.1 spec + auto-generated TS SDK + 3 CI drift gates; (5) **infra-долги Cycle 3 cleanup**: 17 stale `F401` imports + 11 `Test*` class collisions + payload SIGNATURES drift guard (3 regression tests) + apktool drift root-cause investigation + read-only catalog session fixture (защита от любой будущей mid-run mutation) + 5-case regression gate (chmod check + sign-CLI verify × 3 catalogs); (6) **capstone**: coverage matrix 12 → **14 contracts** (C13 signature-mtime-stability × 185 файлов + C14 tool-yaml-version-field-presence × 157 tools, +342 параметрических кейсов), 157 / 157 tool YAML'ов получили `version: "1.0.0"` field + полный re-sign Ed25519, `docs/tool-catalog.md` regenerated с новой `### Image coverage` section, Cycle 4 sign-off отчёт + Cycle 5 carry-over backlog (7 primed tasks ARG-041..ARG-047).
